At noon we returned to camp for lunch and again birded the grounds.  The large fruiting trees above camp and smaller shrubs around the grounds provided ample fruit and flowers for an assortment of guans, chachalacas, hummingbirds, tanagers and even a few cotingas.  In the afternoon we took the trail down the Rio Seteganti and as in the morning, found an antswarm, which was very productive. Unfortunately by 16:00 it began to rain and by the time we returned to camp it was raining very hard. Late in the afternoon it finally stopped raining and we were able to bird the airstrip for about a half-hour before dinner. I was very pleased at the quality of our meals at Cana and given the difficulty and lack of good equipment in the kitchen it was amazing the food was as good as it was.  At about mid-night it started raining again and continued, sometimes with hard driving rain that awoke us several times during the night. ----Other observers: Brian Daniels, Dave De Sante, Pete Ginsberg, Dean Vanier, Tom Wurster.		obs27049	Peter	Ginsburg	S6567286	eBird - Traveling  Count	EBIRD	480	5		6	1	G177321	1	0

That morning we caught a Violet-headed Hummingbird, Rufous-cheeked Hummingbird and Olive-striped Flycatcher with the same reaction from the others in our group as in the previous day. I have banded over 25,000 birds in my life and I never cease to marvel at what birds look like in the hand.  While handling the birds I missed the Tooth-billed Hummingbird the rest of our group saw at camp and that turned out to be the last opportunity I would have to see this specialty of the Cerro Pirre. We left Explorers Inn at 3:30 a.m. to hike to Cochachoca Lagoon and arrive before dawn. We then took a small canoe out onto the lagoon, listened to owls & potoos, and watched dawn arive with flights of pigeons & parrots. Just a marvelous experience..... We stayed on lagoon until 9 a.m. (photos of Agami Heron, screamer, etc; heard Long-billed Woodcreeper, yet another potential lifer not included on the checklist) and then hiked in terra firma until early afternoon, returning back to Explorers Inn by 4 p.m.  Nice weather.
